#Architecture
===============================================================================================================
# Working
Only android and iOS apps from mult brands call Cariad Services
Cariad then call rest of the services like VCF to get data and store the results in Cariad system
Apps then keep polling /pending_action Cariad service to get data
Mostly all are working in Async way

Megatron = K8t cluster system

Core Services = Old Legacy services which has not been converted into new system yet
               Core services written in Kotlin
               Core - User related Kotlin

Vehicles Services = Written in 'Go' language. Core is slowly converting into 'Go'
              Vehicle service - VIN Go

BFF dont track record for Veh reg and deregistation. VCF send us details and we fwd it to user app. with VIN +Userid combination

# 6 Services
IDK Proxy Service              /login/v1/idk    For login and authentication
Vehicle Service                /vehicle/v1      The API allow any given app User to query information about their vehicle or control their vehicle remotely.
Vehicle Image Service          /media/v2        The API allow provide vehicle images for a given VIN
User Service                   /                The API provides access to the market related configuration and user data
Navigation Service             /navigation/v1   The API allows any given car owner to use navigation functionalities
Vehicle Notifications Service  /notification/v1 For App users to subscribe and unsubscribe for notifications on mobiles
AAZS Proxy Service                              for Audi: Track User logins (for Audi only)
MNP Notification Servie                         for Audi: Push notification to Kafka, backend etc
Google Static Maps Service
Gamify Service
Dealer API       (CoreApi)     /dealers/v1      Help to search dealers by coordinates and distance and to update the cache
Login API   Deprecated, Use IDK Proxy Service   /user-login/v1/consent/
Mobile API (BFF)  (CoreApi)                     For backward compatibility for Flutter App. Will be depricated once Android app goes live

===============================================================================================================
New Relic General
===============================================================================================================
- New Relic install its Agents into the Servers which keep sending information to New Relic
- New Relic have their own DBs which store all the data sent by Agents
- Agent can be configured via newrelic.xml configuration file present on Server to be monitored

APM: Application Performance Monitoring
Other Similar tools: Grafana, Kibana, Datadog

# ApDex: Application performance Index (Shd be 1)
T: Threshold Time to Response to a Request  (Apdex T)
R: Actual Response Time to a Req

Satisfied case     R <= T
Tolerated case     T < R < 4T
Frustrated case    R > 4T

              Satisfied Req Count + (Tolerated Req Count/2)
Apdex Index = ---------------------------------
                          Total Req Count

Apdex = 1 Best case
New Relic Dashboard > Settings > Application > Appdex T > Define T e.g. 1 sec(For Backend server) (For Web Browser value can be 6 sec)
'Appdex T' need to be defined for different project and New Relic calculate Apdex accordingly
'Apdex T' can also be set based on backend, web browser, country specific etc

Apdex category:
1. End User: Consider front end loading speed
2. App Server: Consider only backend server speed


#NRQL : New Relic Query Language
Q: How to chose correct 'Appdex T' value as it can impact New Relic graphs
If its too small then lots of alert comes unnecessary. If its too big then no alert will come.

New Relic suggest get response time of 90% of your existing request and set that number as 'Apdex T'
Dashboard > Insights
Select percentile(duration, 90) FROM Transaction where appId=12345
return 0.7 sec
So this value can be set as 'Appdex T' for backend servers


# How to handle 3rd party services
Sometimes page is slow because of 3rd party apis
Dashboard > Monitoring > External Services

# Profiling
How threads are doing, what block causing performance issues etc
We need to start profiling on server for limited time where Agents take performance information

Q: How to start profiling in New Relic
Dashboard > Events > Thread Profiler > Select Server > Select time like 5min, 10 min > Start Profiling

Q: How many Server running my application
Dashboard > Events > Thread Profiler > Here we get list of all server

# Alerts
Dashboard Menu > Alerts
Create Policy > Set Rules for Alerts

Violations:
Dashboard > Alerts > Incidents > Violations >

#How to start with Postman
1. Select BFF API Folder > Authorization Tab > Get New Access Toekn button > Enter username and password > Use Token button
2. Vehicle service > "Vehicles for User V2" API > Run
  Note: Make sure this API > Tests Tab contains following script which will set first Primary VIN in variables or first VIN in case Prim is not present

// test status code
pm.test("Status code is 200", function () {
  pm.response.to.have.status(200);
});

// extract vin
pm.collectionVariables.unset("vin")
const requestJson = pm.response.json()
let length = requestJson.data.length
for(var i = 0; i < requestJson.data.length; i++ ){
    let role = requestJson.data[i].role
    if (role == "PRIMARY_USER") {
        console.log("First PRIMARY_USER VIN Set")
        pm.collectionVariables.set("vin", requestJson.data[i].vin);
        break
    }
}

// if no primary user found, use first vin
let savedVin = pm.collectionVariables.get("vin")
if (savedVin == undefined) {
    console.log("First Non PRIMARY_USER VIN Set")
    pm.collectionVariables.set("vin", requestJson.data[0].vin);
}

  Imp: Copy access_token | user_token is same as access token | some times postman dont save it into user_token, so do it manually
  var token = pm.request.auth.oauth2.get('accessToken');
  pm.collectionVariables.set("user_token", token);

  Hit same Api "Get User Token API" request and get response
  Search for PRIMARY_USER > copy vin number

2. Go to BFF API folder > Variables > Save vin number for all APIs

#Pre-setup for External APIs
Note: For external api testing, BFF "Get User Token" api is not required to run
1. Select Env: External Sand VW EMEA or any other
2. Go to External API > IDK Collection
3. Run all 5 API in sequence: GET > GET > POST > POST > POST
   1. Get User Token : Auth > Clear Cache > Get New Access Token >Login with correct user > Hit using Send button
   2. Get User Info
   3. Service Token : Select Access Token w/o "" > Right Click > Set External > Service Token
   4. Personalised Access Token (PAT): Select Access Token w/o "" > Right Click > Set External > Personalized Token
   5. GDC Token

 SB EMEA	Rst.approval@gmail.com	(RSt4Approval)

Note:
For VCF: all above 5 api need to run
PAT and BFF API > User token are almost same
    PAT used for external apis like VDS, VDBS
    User token used for BFF Apis

For VDBS: top 4 req
    userid need to be correct
    Get User Token > access token > jwt.io > sub (userid)

Core vs User Service

GET 200 https://sb.emea.bff.cariad.digital/user/v1/legaltextconsents/published?serviceids=elli&country=de&language=de

User version=latest with & without

GET https://sb.emea.bff.cariad.digital/user/v1/legaltextconsents/published?serviceids=elli&country=de&language=de&version=latest

User service Mandatory check | 400 in case country or language or both missing
GET https://sb.emea.bff.cariad.digital/user/v1/legaltextconsents/published?serviceids=elli&language=de&version=latest
GET https://sb.emea.bff.cariad.digital/user/v1/legaltextconsents/published?serviceids=elli&country=de&version=latest

#Single Timer
Both should present (backward compatibility)

departureDateTime  : present (ignore)
departureDateTimeLocal : present (ignore)

timer.singleTimer.startDateTime : missing (ignore)
timer.singleTimer.targetDateTime : present

timer.singleTimer.startDateTimeLocal : missing (ignore)
timer.singleTimer.targetDateTimeLocal : present

occuringOn : present


#Recurring Timer
departureTime: present (ignore)
departureTimeLocal: present (ignore)

timer.recurringTimer.startTime  : missing (ignore)
timer.recurringTimer.targetTime : present

timer.recurringTimer.startTimeLocal : missing (ignore)
timer.recurringTimer.targetTimeLocal: present

timer.recurringTimer.recurringOn     : present      [mondays:true, tuesdays:true...... with "s"]
timer.recurringTimer.repetitionDays  : present      [array: monday, tuesday...... w/o "s"]

POST /vehicle/lead/{vin}
criticality enum 0 to 5 int

0 -> No prior data exists to notify about any change. 1 -> status OK 2 -> Predictive warning in advance 3 -> presently Undefined (does not exist in models) 4 -> It is time to change the part/repair something and recommend to go to the workshop for the part replacement 5 -> Safety relavent or when warnings have been ignored for 'X'number of days. Recommended to go to the workshop for part replacement

https://docs.emea.bff.cariad.digital/vehicles#tag/PredictiveMaintenance/operation/CreateLead          v1 missing in docs

Case 1: Valid Values
valid cid = 200
valid ftid = 200

Case 2: Invalid Values
Invalid CID= 502
Invalid FTID=502

Case 3: Sending both value together
valid cid + ftid = 200
invalid cid + ftid = 400

Case 4: No cid or ftid
400

Requirement:
#Success Logs
  - keep incoming request logs with request and response bodies | Dont remove
  - drop the outgoing calls completely
  - remove in_progress logs for callbacks.
#Non-Success Logs
  - Keep both incoming and outgoing
  - remove in_progress logs for callbacks.
